# Active lane dispatch claims — cross-agent coordination ledger

**MANDATORY for ALL agents (Claude, codex, future):** Before dispatching ANY training, eval, or remote-GPU job, READ this file FIRST and APPEND a claim row. Check for conflicts on the same `lane_id` within the past 24h.

If you find an active conflicting claim:
- Do NOT dispatch
- Either coordinate with the other agent (via this file's notes column) or pick a different lane
- Document the conflict resolution

If you find a STALE claim (status=provisioning/training but timestamp > 24h ago and no completion):
- Mark it `stale_assumed_dead` with a note
- You may then claim the lane

When your dispatch completes (success or fail):
- Append a terminal row with the same `lane_id` and `instance/job_id` via `tools/claim_lane_dispatch.py claim --force --status completed_...` or `--status failed_...`; the helper treats a newer terminal row as closing the matching older nonterminal row.

## Lane ID convention

Use the canonical lane name from `.omx/state/lane_registry.json`. Examples:
- `q_faithful` — Q-FAITHFUL JointFrameGenerator retrain
- `lane_g_v3` — Lane G v3 baseline
- `lane_owv3_0120_stack` — OWv3 0120 orthogonal stack
- `lane_sjkl_v1` — Wave-Ω-1 SJ-KL basis
- `lane_qzs3_qp1_packer` — Wave-1 QZS3+QP1 packer
- `lane_line_search_pose_refinement` — Wave-1.5 line-search

## Status values

- `provisioning` — instance booting, code uploading
- `bootstrapping` — uv/ffmpeg/etc installing
- `training` — main training loop running
- `eval` — contest-CUDA auth eval running
- `harvest` — pulling artifacts back to local
- `completed_score=X` — done, contest-CUDA score X landed
- `failed_<short_reason>` — dispatch failed pre-completion
- `preempted` — chip provider preempted
- `cancelled` — claim withdrawn (operator chose different lane)
- `stale_assumed_dead` — heartbeat > 24h stale, claim auto-released

## Heartbeat protocol (informal)

Long-running dispatches (> 1h) should append a `# heartbeat` line every 1h with the agent name + dispatch_id + last-observed remote state (e.g., epoch number, log line). This is BEST-EFFORT; the canonical heartbeat lives on the remote instance per CLAUDE.md Check 41.

## Why this exists

2026-05-01 ~23:50 UTC user reported possible Q-FAITHFUL dispatch conflict between Claude (H100 SXM via Vast.ai) and codex (Lightning). No formal cross-agent coordination existed. This file is the Level 1 minimal fix. Level 2 (helper script + STRICT preflight) will land after the current Q-FAITHFUL run completes.
